``Mac (mak). A Gaelic Word signifying Son, and prefixed to many Surnames, as Mac Donald, Mac Grigor & C. It is synonymous with Son fem, magattes (G. magd, a maid)'' - The Imperial Dictionary of the English Language (Vol.III, p.91).
